## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population size P and time t, which is the fundamental setup of population dynamics ODE models. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth with possible temporal modulation.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Malthusian growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (exponential growth, no density dependence)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth decelerating logarithmically near capacity)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Strong Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with critical minimum population threshold)
- Weak Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 * (1 - c2 * P) (cooperative growth at low density)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (saturating per-capita growth)
- Seasonally forced logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (logistic with periodic environment)
- Time-varying carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t)) (logistic with shifting capacity)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (flexible sigmoidal growth curve)
- Quadratic density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (polynomial density effects)
- Harvesting model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (logistic growth with constant removal)
- Ratio-dependent decay: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 / (1 + c2 * P) (growth with saturating competition)
- Exponential decline model: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * P) (exponentially modified per-capita rate)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent negative feedback → quadratic term -c*P^2 or rational form P/(1+c*P) representing intraspecific competition
- Allee effects (positive density dependence at low P) → cubic polynomial in P or product of two linear factors in P
- Carrying capacity structure → factor of form (1 - P/K) ensuring zero growth at equilibrium population
- Gompertz-type deceleration → logarithmic dependence log(K/P) giving asymmetric growth curve
- Seasonal or periodic environmental forcing → multiplicative sinusoidal modulation sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) on growth rate
- Immigration/emigration → additive constant term independent of P in the growth rate equation
- Cooperative/group effects at low density → fractional power P^c with 0<c<1 or sigmoidal response in P
- Multiple equilibria structure → polynomial in P with roots corresponding to stable/unstable fixed points
- Time-dependent parameters → coefficients that are explicit functions of t (linear, exponential, or periodic)
- Predation saturation → Holling type II functional response c*P/(1+c*P) subtracted from growth

- Second term: `0.11424*P - 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*P)`
- Third term: `0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)`

Combining: `-0.002807*P² + 0.22848*P - 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*P) + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)`

So GT = `c_a*P² + c_b*P + c_c*P*exp(c_d*P) + c_e*P*exp(c_f*t)`

where c_a = -0.002807, c_b = 0.22848, c_c = -0.11424, c_d = -0.08368, c_e = 0.11424, c_f = -0.08368.

The GT has four distinct structural components:
1. `P²` term
2. `P` term

## GT Analysis

The GT expression is:
$$f(t,P) = 0.11424(1 - P/40.698)P + 0.11424(1 - e^{-0.08368P})P + 0.11424 \cdot P \cdot e^{-0.08368t}$$

Let me expand this:
$$= 0.11424P - 0.11424P^2/40.698 + 0.11424P - 0.11424P \cdot e^{-0.08368P} + 0.11424P \cdot e^{-0.08368t}$$

$$= -0.002807P^2 + 0.22848P - 0.11424P \cdot e^{-0.08368P} + 0.11424P \cdot e^{-0.08368t}$$

The GT has these basis functions in terms of P and t:
1. $P^2$ term
2. $P$ term  
3. $P \cdot e^{-cP}$ term (exponential in P)
4. $P \cdot e^{-ct}$ term (exponential in t)

This is crucial: the GT contains both $P \cdot e^{-cP}$ and $P \cdot e^{-ct}$ terms. Any matching candidate must be able to reproduce these.

Let me now check each candidate systematically. I'll focus on whether each candidate has the right basis functions.

**Key requirements:**
- Must have $P^2$ term ✓ (most candidates have this)
- Must have $P$ term ✓
- Must have $P \cdot \exp(cP)$ term (exponential in P times P)
- Must have $P \cdot \exp(ct)$ term (exponential in t times P) — or equivalent

Let me check candidates that have both exp(P) and exp(t) type terms:

### Candidate 4: $P^2c_0 + Pc_1 + c_2\log(c_3t+1) + c_4t + c_5/(c_6t+c_7) + c_8$
